			</div>			<header class="entry-header" aria-label="Content">
				<h1 class="entry-title" itemprop="headline">Action Verbs: List of 50 Common Action Verbs with Pictures</h1>			</header>

		<div class="entry-content" itemprop="text">
			<p>Action Verbs! Useful list of action verbs in English with pictures and example sentences. <span style="font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;">Verbs are vital in any language and English is no different, however there are often so many that it can become very confusing. For this reason we have broken the English verbs down into more manageable chunks. In this section, you will be looking at verbs that are used to describe an action. These verbs will help you in being able to construct a sentence and will get you well on your way to having a rich vocabulary of English verbs.</span></p>

<h2><span class="ez-toc-section" id="Verbs_with_Pictures_for_Kids"></span><strong>Verbs with Pictures for Kids</strong><span class="ez-toc-section-end"></span></h2>
<p>Learn useful <a href="https://7esl.com/english-verbs/" data-lasso-id="2105">verbs list</a> commonly used in English with <a href="https://7esl.com/common-verbs/" data-lasso-id="2106">verbs pictures</a> for kids.</p>
<ul>
<li>List of <a href="https://7esl.com/action-verbs-vocabulary/" data-lasso-id="2107">action verbs</a> with images.</li>
<li><a href="https://7esl.com/classroom-verbs-vocabulary/" data-lasso-id="2108">Classroom verbs</a> vocabulary in English.</li>
<li><a href="https://7esl.com/restaurant-verbs-vocabulary/" data-lasso-id="2109">Restaurant verbs</a> in English.</li>
<li><a href="https://7esl.com/housework-and-repair-verbs/" data-lasso-id="2110">Household chores</a> with pictures in English.</li>
<li>List of <a href="https://7esl.com/daily-routines/" data-lasso-id="2111">daily routines</a> in English.</li>
<li>Body <a href="https://7esl.com/verbs-of-body-movement/" data-lasso-id="2112">movement verbs</a> with images in English.</li>
<li><a href="https://7esl.com/action-words/" data-lasso-id="2113">Action words</a> with pictures.</li>
<li>List of <a href="https://7esl.com/cooking-verbs/" data-lasso-id="2114">cooking verbs</a> in English.</li>
<li><a href="https://7esl.com/sport-and-exercise-actions-vocabulary/" data-lasso-id="2115">Sport words</a> and exercise actions vocabulary words.</li>
</ul>
